 <p data-pid="GVTEdFCy"><b>　玛法里奥成功的指引兽人女战士索拉·萨鲁法尔替自己解除禁锢灵魂的梦魇法术，接着回到世界树泰达希尔击倒成为梦魇爪牙的徒弟范达尔·鹿盔，净化了泰达希尔。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5c029d354290bd44c44344a4b2b404d7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="580" data-rawheight="773" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-5c029d354290bd44c44344a4b2b404d7" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-ccde59fd7c62eaaf816b54bfe063b5e6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="580" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-5c029d354290bd44c44344a4b2b404d7_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   范达尔·鹿盔
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ePZSiDzN"><b>　玛法里奥引导众德鲁伊和其他许多英雄组成反抗军对抗梦魇之王哈维斯，联手同时击溃哈维斯的实体形态和梦境形态</b>，翡翠梦魇大举消退至梦境中的奥恩裂隙，<b>梦魇之战结束。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="RAUlvOqx"><b>红龙女王阿莱克丝塔萨和绿龙女王伊瑟拉为了感激凡人在梦魇之战的贡献，对世界之树泰达希尔施加了龙王的祝福。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f1e107c8e7b7c0e3f16d7268edd6a3d3_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="500" data-rawheight="375" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-f1e107c8e7b7c0e3f16d7268edd6a3d3" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2208ba21552754ed90c17eebb1b40856_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="500" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-f1e107c8e7b7c0e3f16d7268edd6a3d3_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="b38deU9z"><b>　侏儒王吉尔宾·梅卡托克执行“</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E8%25AF%25BA%25E8%258E%25AB%25E7%2591%259E%25E6%25A0%25B9" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">诺莫瑞根</a><b>行动”的战斗计划</b>，意图夺回被辐射污染、被穴居怪和背叛者占领的诺莫瑞根。<b>然而最后却失败</b>，<b>仅夺回诺莫瑞根的地表区域，城市和中心区依旧被占领。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="K4X3FPbC"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%259A%2597%25E7%259F%259B%25E5%25B7%25A8%25E9%25AD%2594" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">暗矛巨魔</a><b>酋长</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%25B2%2583%25E9%2587%2591" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">沃金</a><b>进行回音群岛夺回计划，成功的打倒背叛者扎拉赞恩，光复了自己的家园。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-95fc69f838bbf034d18ec17a93b534d1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="500" data-rawheight="281" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-95fc69f838bbf034d18ec17a93b534d1" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-fb2b9896b08f93d35ce60163375f8868_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="500" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-95fc69f838bbf034d18ec17a93b534d1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   回音群岛
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="_9FMGWvT"><b>　　狼人诅咒在</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%2590%2589%25E5%25B0%2594%25E5%25B0%25BC%25E6%2596%25AF" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">吉尔尼斯</a><b>王国境内失控，造成包含国王吉恩在内的大部分人民都被诅咒感染而变成狼人，吉尔尼斯都城被狼人攻陷。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-8bf7cae8338f4ab7bd512abd9acb40d3_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="800" data-rawheight="347" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-8bf7cae8338f4ab7bd512abd9acb40d3" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-a19a5ff7dfb4c442d367ef55d21a04e7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="800" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8bf7cae8338f4ab7bd512abd9acb40d3_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="6tvwzxMN"><b>黑龙王死亡之翼</b>开始进行一连串毁灭艾泽拉斯的计划，<b>元素之灵纷纷感受到灭世的危机而到处肆虐，造成全世界天灾不断。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-ad7acfcdbbfd3bde95b7c9b6a1c9c746_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="580" data-rawheight="348" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-ad7acfcdbbfd3bde95b7c9b6a1c9c746" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f858820cc094899dc04b797be664a39d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="580" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-ad7acfcdbbfd3bde95b7c9b6a1c9c746_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="lVf5ZOjR"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%25A4%25A7%25E5%259C%25B0%25E4%25B9%258B%25E7%258E%25AF" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">大地之环</a><b>首领穆恩·大地之怒肃清组织内上古之神的仆人之后重新整顿议会，并且招募蛮锤矮人萨满加入，以对抗上古之神和暮光之锤教派为目标。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-f42c0498d279a97e5836ec23cc309e86_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="335" data-rawheight="465" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-f42c0498d279a97e5836ec23cc309e86" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f16bdc982b4c4e64588258a7b0a1c60f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="335">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="V69_WUS_"><b>天灾持续侵袭艾泽拉斯，其中一场大地震重创矮人的卡兹莫丹王国，国王麦格尼·铜须决定使用来自奥杜尔的石板所记载的仪式拯救自己的国家，却就此化为钻石。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-ae6fddd80a8708ddbd61126e4b5b5f8b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1680" data-rawheight="1050" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-ae6fddd80a8708ddbd61126e4b5b5f8b" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-36fb569127108523bb8784782dd2cb9a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1680" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-ae6fddd80a8708ddbd61126e4b5b5f8b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="J_LxY2me"><b>　　部落大酋长萨尔为了查明造成天灾不断的真相而前往外域学习更进一步的萨满之道，临走前将部落大酋长职位交予加尔鲁什·地狱咆哮担任。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-278e50434e096bc7df16e8a1e6d67d24_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="800" data-rawheight="600" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-278e50434e096bc7df16e8a1e6d67d24" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-cfa4fa20ffcbe2ea78e5b226ad38b049_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="800" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-278e50434e096bc7df16e8a1e6d67d24_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   加尔鲁什·地狱咆哮
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="JKgNQ0Qn"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E8%258C%2589%25E8%2589%25BE%25E6%258B%2589%25C2%25B7%25E9%2593%259C%25E9%25A1%25BB" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">茉艾拉·铜须</a>公主带领部分的<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E9%25BB%2591%25E9%2593%2581%25E7%259F%25AE%25E4%25BA%25BA" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">黑铁矮人</a>回归卡兹莫丹王国并继任新女王，同时下令铁炉堡全城戒严。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-255485252961743565af066f86503e7c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="400" data-rawheight="530" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-255485252961743565af066f86503e7c" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6080bc4e55b0820fe384edfeb659fb8a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="400">
  <figcaption>
   茉艾拉·铜须（看着还好吧。。其实。。。）
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-72c72d642924a36be2b5818360e47b89_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="320" data-rawheight="500" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-72c72d642924a36be2b5818360e47b89" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-df18edeeaa4524f2dfcc53df39358796_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="320">
  <figcaption>
   其实长这样
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="BazD8JET"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%259A%25AE%25E5%2585%2589%25E4%25B9%258B%25E9%2594%25A4" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">暮光之锤</a><b>教派屠杀德鲁伊和谈会议的代表然后嫁祸给加尔鲁什，导致牛头人大族长</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%2587%25AF%25E6%2581%25A9%25C2%25B7%25E8%25A1%2580%25E8%25B9%2584" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">凯恩·血蹄</a><b>发起挑战大酋长的生死决斗。恐怖图腾部族的首领玛加萨趁机下毒造成凯恩被加尔鲁什杀死，然后再发动政变控制住雷霆崖。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-32362990ed355cc37fd71e127e8175c2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="438" data-rawheight="427" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-32362990ed355cc37fd71e127e8175c2" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-ff27a7403d919deb297566e92821eead_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="438" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-32362990ed355cc37fd71e127e8175c2_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   右边那个拿着法杖的是 玛加萨
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="Ru_FEl0v"><b>凯恩之子贝恩前往拜访人类大法师吉安娜寻求协助，并且大举征召推翻玛加萨统治的反抗势力，在诸多勇士的帮忙下成功的夺回雷霆崖之后永远放逐玛加萨和继续追随她的恐怖图腾牛头人。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-4ccc1882aed3308eadf7a52a4a5cf602_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1003" data-rawheight="793" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-4ccc1882aed3308eadf7a52a4a5cf602" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-884fdc2addea79f6b11186761daa362e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1003" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-4ccc1882aed3308eadf7a52a4a5cf602_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="w6RCVg11"><b>暴风王国国王瓦里安带兵潜入铁炉堡意图刺杀矮人女王茉艾拉，不过遭到王子安度因出手阻止，暗杀事件遂而转变成矮人王国的政治剧变，蛮锤矮人正式回归卡兹莫丹王国，王位依旧由茉艾拉继承，但统治权则交由矮人三族共同治理，是为三锤议会。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-ef3b571e1463fa6546165a7a96a6c7df_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="845" data-rawheight="1199" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-ef3b571e1463fa6546165a7a96a6c7df" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-8268d8a8968ecee229bb7f9000ffca64_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="845" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-ef3b571e1463fa6546165a7a96a6c7df_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ce5WmdPz"><b>死亡之翼击碎世界之柱，强硬连结元素位面到艾泽拉斯，异空间的强硬撕扯引发继上古之战的天崩地裂之后重创艾泽拉斯最可怕的灾难，即大灾变。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3d598b25821470756e06be8bbfd99e80_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1600" data-rawheight="1131" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-3d598b25821470756e06be8bbfd99e80" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bace05d8fbcd0ed89cdf3f83b5e26616_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-3d598b25821470756e06be8bbfd99e80_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-1aab628d65bc84a77e7db270369a04c5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="505" data-rawheight="1000" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-1aab628d65bc84a77e7db270369a04c5" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-ae24519d1c9052cdb653dd717e07d737_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="505" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1aab628d65bc84a77e7db270369a04c5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="sv1pPW1S">　萨尔与伴侣阿格拉带着亲信部队出发前往大漩涡，为拯救艾泽拉斯而行。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-24403647c27df6a36e7b2ad49829ebe5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="500" data-rawheight="332" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-24403647c27df6a36e7b2ad49829ebe5" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-fd26772d06df10b354b2b7fdc0fbef5b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="500" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-24403647c27df6a36e7b2ad49829ebe5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <hr>
 <p data-pid="5d4T8Ix4"><b>30</b></p>
 <p data-pid="3T365KQf"><b> 大酋长加尔鲁什以征服全艾泽拉斯为目标下令对联盟全面宣战。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="wsaPj6wC"><b>被遗忘者攻入饱受狼人诅咒肆虐的吉尔尼斯王国，暗夜精灵在玛法里奥的指示下出兵协助吉尔尼斯王国控制诅咒和对抗部落。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="k_ioI1Du"><b>吉尔尼斯暂时击退部落，</b>但是面对战争冲突不断与残破不堪的家园，大部分的居民撤退到<b>暗夜精灵的达纳苏斯城暂居。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/timg_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="timg" class="content_image">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="DyoUHUky"><b>部落全面进攻暗夜精灵领地，联盟召开领袖高峰会，暴风王国国王瓦里安成为联盟对抗部落的战争总指挥官，吉尔尼斯王国正式重回联盟。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="FKbj1nu8"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%25AD%25BB%25E4%25BA%25A1%25E4%25B9%258B%25E7%25BF%25BC" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">死亡之翼</a><b>降临科赞岛引发火山爆发，大量锈水财阀的地精搭乘避难船逃亡。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-0e5c1b8a728801f00407b7ccde8a5e3c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="550" data-rawheight="283" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-0e5c1b8a728801f00407b7ccde8a5e3c" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4c0e186aadeb3fdcd497b638bdbbf481_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="550" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0e5c1b8a728801f00407b7ccde8a5e3c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   科赞岛
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ZQPeRGK5"><b>萨尔和</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E9%2598%25BF%25E6%25A0%25BC%25E6%258B%2589" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">阿格拉</a><b>航行往大漩涡的船被联盟拦截，锈水财阀的避难船也被卷入击沉</b>。<b>地精们因缘际会之下救出萨尔并击退联盟追兵，在萨尔的引导下加里维克斯的奴隶计划被迫放弃，变成他带领锈水财阀加入部落。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-760111cbd34eb4ffb818f9216aa448db_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="550" data-rawheight="810" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-760111cbd34eb4ffb818f9216aa448db" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6f65bab3f763adabe84100e485491be7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="550" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-760111cbd34eb4ffb818f9216aa448db_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   加里维克斯
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="iYyPeccH"><b>红龙的净化黑龙计划成功，纯净的黑龙蛋诞生，日后孵出未受到污染的黑龙</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%258B%2589%25E5%25B8%258C%25E5%25A5%25A5" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">拉希奥</a><b>。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-b520bd484c58897026ac38f145463c56_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="550" data-rawheight="278" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-b520bd484c58897026ac38f145463c56" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-fbe346d881faaf70170338ce503d374b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="550" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-b520bd484c58897026ac38f145463c56_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   拉希奥
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="iex8uwRp"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%25B5%25B7%25E5%258A%25A0%25E5%25B0%2594%25E5%25B1%25B1" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">海加尔山</a><b>战役中诸多半神靠着大灾变的异位面不稳定而重生</b>，<b>火元素军团暂时被绿龙军团与玛法里奥统帅的</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%25A1%259E%25E7%25BA%25B3%25E9%2587%258C%25E5%25A5%25A5%25E8%25AE%25AE%25E4%25BC%259A" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">塞纳里奥议会</a><b>击败而退回火焰之地。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-efa297641edf7c827fb9020a3f10c037_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1269" data-rawheight="642" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-efa297641edf7c827fb9020a3f10c037" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-794318b678e546b08b550b2636de2382_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1269" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-efa297641edf7c827fb9020a3f10c037_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   火焰之地
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="J1PXatVj"><b>水元素位面深渊之喉被纳迦与无面者入侵，水元素之王奈普图隆战败被俘，就此下落不明。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-bc044d0e34f3f8031d7875b7a0f46575_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="500" data-rawheight="343" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-bc044d0e34f3f8031d7875b7a0f46575" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a204a83589a46f17d7fb835555983fb6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="500" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-bc044d0e34f3f8031d7875b7a0f46575_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="oa8CkWul"><b>　　大地之环与土元素之王</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%25A1%259E%25E6%258B%2589%25E8%25B5%259E%25E6%2581%25A9" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">塞拉赞恩</a><b>合作，共同修复修复世界之柱，将暮光之锤与上古之神的势力从土元素位面深岩之洲驱逐。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-07061506dbc6d5ea6917aad1213fc119_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="602" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-07061506dbc6d5ea6917aad1213fc119" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-15144d37ea1cd10ba3efda8c3ad366b7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-07061506dbc6d5ea6917aad1213fc119_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   魔兽世界四元素领主之一石母塞拉赞恩
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="bHRG2wC7"><b>　大探险家布莱恩破坏奥丹姆内的世界重塑装置，免除了此装置被死亡之翼和上古之神控制的风险。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0d3491429491e5840e102980e57b2f27_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1680" data-rawheight="1050" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-0d3491429491e5840e102980e57b2f27" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a06a774f0bc5b4d6d330501eecbaacf8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1680" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-0d3491429491e5840e102980e57b2f27_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="8r38Pf2D"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%2589%2598%25E7%25BB%25B4%25E5%25B0%2594" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">托维尔</a><b>三族爆发激烈内战，最终由拉穆卡恒部族取得胜利，并和冒险者共同合作，进攻风元素位面天空之墙，击杀风元素之王</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%25A5%25A5%25E6%258B%2589%25E5%259F%25BA%25E5%25B0%2594" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">奥拉基尔</a><b>。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-fd011d04f1d8b7e9597934f351989249_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="550" data-rawheight="344" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-fd011d04f1d8b7e9597934f351989249" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-8fc56a37c0217efb9f32df4b46d69b71_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="550" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fd011d04f1d8b7e9597934f351989249_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="OwTDwems"><b>　　部落与联盟分别进攻暮光高地，各获得龙喉氏族与蛮锤部族的协助，击溃暮光之锤的要塞暮光堡垒。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="Y4yUjGon"><b>赞达拉部族由于赞达拉本岛在大灾变中毁灭，因此召集其他巨魔同胞，意图团结所有巨魔以重建其古老的帝国荣光，但暗矛部族依旧选择留在部落。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-d49d1ad1231e00eb2bf77fc87e3994af_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="459" data-rawheight="292" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-d49d1ad1231e00eb2bf77fc87e3994af" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-522a615c54f2ea762c93694883f9b383_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="459" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d49d1ad1231e00eb2bf77fc87e3994af_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="n_1_AvT6"><b>　　萨尔进入时光之穴的迷宫，成功的找回失踪多年的青铜龙王诺兹多姆，并揭开永恒龙军团乃是堕落的青铜龙真相。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="nkRVqIiV"><b>　每430年才一次的双月相拥天象，蓝龙一族群聚魔枢，萨尔协助</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%258D%25A1%25E9%259B%25B7%25E8%258B%259F%25E6%2596%25AF" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">卡雷苟斯</a><b>取得新任蓝龙王之位。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-bd36c9ec3345ab9b65c9b80d3c2d972a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="300" data-rawheight="265" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-bd36c9ec3345ab9b65c9b80d3c2d972a" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1f13ed7dbd6bf67e2905596843af958e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="300">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="o6UvfJeu"><b>萨尔协助巨龙军团重新团结，龙眠联军再度重聚，击败并封印死亡之翼与奈法利安的秘密武器“龙王的终暮”：多彩五头龙</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%2585%258B%25E6%25B4%259B%25E7%258E%259B%25E5%259B%25BE%25E6%2596%25AF" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">克洛玛图斯</a><b>。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1503f6af11ddfaf876bc500c8b123638_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="340" data-rawheight="454" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-1503f6af11ddfaf876bc500c8b123638" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0a2955a01e19d500d968f7f0b694bdf0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="340">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="bDUDp0df"><b>塞纳里奥议会攻入火焰之地，击杀火元素之王</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%258B%2589%25E6%25A0%25BC%25E7%25BA%25B3%25E7%25BD%2597%25E6%2596%25AF" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">拉格纳罗斯</a><b>。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f2e3eb8fd3b868abcc3cd409c75fa275_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1440" data-rawheight="900" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-f2e3eb8fd3b868abcc3cd409c75fa275" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3575c9013a441b90555b572b96d544fc_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1440" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f2e3eb8fd3b868abcc3cd409c75fa275_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="jQnBeeB2"><b>　　黑龙王子</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%258B%2589%25E5%25B8%258C%25E5%25A5%25A5" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">拉希奥</a><b>逃脱红龙监控，与秘密的盗贼组织</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%258B%2589%25E6%2596%2587%25E9%259C%258D%25E5%25BE%25B7" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">拉文霍德</a><b>合作，进行铲除艾泽拉斯上所剩的堕落黑龙计划。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-550d4051cca504fe3f6dae923e8c4217_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="510" data-rawheight="225" data-size="normal" data-original-token="v2-550d4051cca504fe3f6dae923e8c4217" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5abaa20a38fea60ef95e02087b86a5b8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="510" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-550d4051cca504fe3f6dae923e8c4217_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   拉文霍德
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ECI8va4K"><b>青铜龙王诺兹多姆冻结上古之战的时间线，暂时从过去借回神器巨龙之魂。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-8d30b3e2a8f64d2aaa3ddaa7d13859ff_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="626" data-rawheight="800" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-8d30b3e2a8f64d2aaa3ddaa7d13859ff" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-27c294b3cbb64d4496792a639fa04a8d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="626" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-8d30b3e2a8f64d2aaa3ddaa7d13859ff_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="XofOnFTg"><b>死亡之翼发动为了执行</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E6%259A%25AE%25E5%2585%2589%25E5%25AE%25A1%25E5%2588%25A4" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">暮光审判</a><b>的最后大战，但却被龙眠联军与来自部落和联盟诸多英雄的联军击败，萨尔驾驭巨龙之魂打退死亡之翼。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a4e4266f1d058c837bdb583d15c29948_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="500" data-rawheight="415" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-a4e4266f1d058c837bdb583d15c29948" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a6695b9daab568b58001f0856b825879_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="500" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a4e4266f1d058c837bdb583d15c29948_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="vs8Zv9Z_"><b>萨尔与四龙王再度联手于大漩涡大战死亡之翼。诸位龙王用尽了所有泰坦赐予的龙王之力而化为凡躯，但也终于彻底消灭死亡之翼。大灾变至此结束，凡人的时代正式开始。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-cc18720ee11cc293a7d42916491712ab_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="450" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-cc18720ee11cc293a7d42916491712ab" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-dd86f346df55429c91e57664cffe7aed_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-cc18720ee11cc293a7d42916491712ab_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <hr>
 <p data-pid="Tjs2m3xN"><b>31-----熊猫人之谜</b></p>
 <p data-pid="3vKekvoc"><b>大酋长</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%258A%25A0%25E5%25B0%2594%25E9%25B2%2581%25E4%25BB%2580" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">加尔鲁什</a><b>指挥部落入侵</b><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//baike.baidu.com/item/%25E5%25A1%259E%25E6%258B%2589%25E6%2591%25A9" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">塞拉摩</a><b>，使用大型毁灭武器炸毁城市，塞拉摩毁灭。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5560f20fd02a09643d4c7a58fae6ad8a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="2412" data-rawheight="933" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-5560f20fd02a09643d4c7a58fae6ad8a" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-cd8d79243803c2c8e3d1a67e282268ce_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="2412" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-5560f20fd02a09643d4c7a58fae6ad8a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-eb282b6aaff7efd2bc7b65135dd2d373_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="537" data-rawheight="429" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-eb282b6aaff7efd2bc7b65135dd2d373" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-b0197f7b994d54ccec72d28331445e3e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="537" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-eb282b6aaff7efd2bc7b65135dd2d373_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="LMB57fvz"><b>　　联盟与部落爆发激烈海战，激战导致双方两败俱伤，残存者尽皆意外的来到迷雾消失的潘达利亚上。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="EzOh7Aib"><b>联盟与部落的残存者将战争延烧到潘达利亚，熊猫人急欲阻止而未果。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="0GWzJYjO"><b>联盟飞船寻天号坠毁于巨龟神真子背上，导致巨龟差点被卷入大漩涡而毁灭。岛上部分熊猫人分别在土水派的艾莎·云歌和火金派的季·火掌的带领下加入联盟部落。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-fab9c691a2cb13b3d0ba167747916672_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="340" data-rawheight="290" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-fab9c691a2cb13b3d0ba167747916672" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-24963273d863aa6c26aef2a19cc8e05e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="340">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="zjwLHGXb"><b>　　潘达利亚上，联盟与部分锦鱼人结盟，部落与猢狲成为盟友。双方激化锦鱼人和猢狲之间的冲突，终至爆发激烈大战，将所有的煞从封印中解放。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-d9d8f7902c48581d0c2df9413a8748b8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="640" data-rawheight="360" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-d9d8f7902c48581d0c2df9413a8748b8" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-9464819e25308dcf92902ebf78054f69_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="640" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d9d8f7902c48581d0c2df9413a8748b8_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-8b7cc3e31c3d89345b42dae8d60070a0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="621" data-rawheight="928" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-8b7cc3e31c3d89345b42dae8d60070a0" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-1691ca9e0c9cea522461a6f3302f540a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="621" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b7cc3e31c3d89345b42dae8d60070a0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="4A2xBV_U"><b>魔古一族在席恩的带领下重新集结，与赞达拉巨魔搭上线，计划趁此再夺统治权，从北岸全面入侵潘达利亚。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f29d8c27b44fdb3ed83e4cfa1fa2d4c7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="800" data-rawheight="600" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-f29d8c27b44fdb3ed83e4cfa1fa2d4c7" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b6d0d5a4bf3a946dee422dc23b6712f4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="800" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f29d8c27b44fdb3ed83e4cfa1fa2d4c7_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="iR6K_7RM"><b>　　部落与联盟舰队纷纷大举出兵潘达利亚，尽皆意图夺取占领此地的丰富资源。熊猫人帝国建国来的最大危机、国家与民族存亡之秋。</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-217451031624ec06b1b84b9dd5185090_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="500" data-rawheight="224" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-217451031624ec06b1b84b9dd5185090" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-c99d04550642d680d20b235065643e32_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="500" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-217451031624ec06b1b84b9dd5185090_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <hr>
 <p data-pid="UlQxr5BW"><b>32</b></p>
 <p data-pid="I5sAvbhX"><b>熊猫人为保证帝国的安全，只能对部落 联盟和魔古一族正式宣战，并与大战之后的锦鱼人和猢狲的残余结盟。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="RTy5wNML"><b>魔古从北岸登陆潘达利亚，部落从东部登陆，联盟从东南部登陆。</b></p>
 <p data-pid="lUbVoVbi"><b>熊猫帝国首领Mojo Dark-Ale带领帝国内的熊猫人积极做战前准备，随时迎战</b>。</p>
